<section class="process-section" id="process">
<div class="container">
<div class="section-head reveal panel-motion-copy">
<div class="section-label">실행 과정</div>
<h2><span style="display:block; font-size:0.48em; font-weight:700; margin-bottom:22px; color:#000000;">실패 없는 성장을 위한 무드애드의</span><span style="display:block; font-size:1em; font-weight:900; color:#18A8F1;">마케팅 로드맵 설계</span></h2>
<p style="font-size:96.8%;">
            투명하게 다 공개해 드립니다. 현장 분석부터 대표 실무진 배정, 광고 최적화,<br/> 실시간 보고와 다음 전략까지,
            실제 매출 흐름에 맞춰 성장을 도와드립니다.
          </p>
</div>

<div class="mobile-process-editorial" aria-label="모바일 실행 과정">
  <article class="mobile-editorial-step reveal-mobile-step" data-step="01">

      <p><strong>Action</strong> 현재 광고 계정 분석 및 온라인 상태를 먼저 정확하게 파악합니다.</p>
      <p><strong>Point</strong> 왜 성과가 멈췄는지, 어디에서 예산이 새고 있는지 데이터를 통해 바로 짚어냅니다.</p>
      <div class="mobile-editorial-tags">
        <span>#계정분석</span><span>#경쟁사파악</span><span>#예산체크</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  </article>

  <div class="mobile-step-connector" aria-hidden="true" data-connector="01-02"><div class="mobile-step-connector-track"></div><div class="mobile-step-connector-orb"></div></div>

        <div class="mobile-editorial-num">STEP 02</div>
      </div>
      <h3>대표 실무진 2:1 전담 배정</h3>
      <p><strong>Action</strong> 진행 사항 안내와 함께 실시간 단톡방을 열고 바로 실행 체계에 들어갑니다.</p>
      <p><strong>Point</strong> 전략가와 디자이너, 두 대표가 직접 뛰는 구조로 진짜 마케팅이 시작됩니다.</p>
      <div class="mobile-editorial-tags">
        <span>#실무진배정</span><span>#실시간소통</span><span>#단톡방운영</span>

      <p><strong>Action</strong> 직접 방문, 상권 분석, 촬영까지 현장에서 필요한 데이터를 수집합니다.</p>
      <p><strong>Point</strong> 책상 위에서 보이지 않는 매출 포인트를 현장에서 직접 확인하고 설계합니다.</p>

      <p><strong>Point</strong> 우리 가게에 맞는 타겟만 정교하게 잡아 예산 낭비를 줄이고 효율을 높입니다.</p>
      <div class="mobile-editorial-tags">

      <h3>실시간 작업 현황 보고</h3>
      <p><strong>Action</strong> 지금 무엇을 진행하고 있는지, 어떤 변화가 있는지 바로 공유드립니다.</p>
      <p><strong>Point</strong> 궁금할 틈 없이 과정을 투명하게 보여드려 믿고 맡길 수 있게 만듭니다.</p>
      <div class="mobile-editorial-tags">
        <span>#실시간보고</span><span>#투명운영</span><span>#현황공유</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  </article>

  <div class="mobile-step-connector" aria-hidden="true" data-connector="05-06"><div class="mobile-step-connector-track"></div><div class="mobile-step-connector-orb"></div></div>

  <article class="mobile-editorial-step reveal-mobile-step" data-step="06">
    <div class="mobile-step-anchor" aria-hidden="true"></div>
    <div class="mobile-step-card">
      <div class="mobile-editorial-head">
        <div class="mobile-editorial-kicker">확장 단계</div>
        <div class="mobile-editorial-num">STEP 06</div>
      </div>
      <h3>성과 분석 &amp; 포스트 전략</h3>
      <p><strong>Action</strong> 현재 성과를 분석하고 다음 달 확장 방향까지 함께 제안합니다.</p>
      <p><strong>Point</strong> 한 번의 운영으로 끝내지 않고 계속 성장할 수 있는 다음 전략까지 이어갑니다.</p>
      <div class="mobile-editorial-tags">
        <span>#성과분석</span><span>#트렌드수집</span><span>#확장전략</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  </article>
</div>

<div class="process-point"><strong>Point:</strong> 왜 성과가 안 나왔는지, 데이터로 구멍 난 예산을 즉시 찾아냅니다.</div>
<div class="process-meta">

<section class="problem-section" id="problem">
<div class="container">

<h2 class="problem-headline" style="letter-spacing:0.2em;"><span class="title-line line-1">하지만, 아셔야 할 게 있습니다.<br/><br/></span><span class="title-line line-2" style="display:block; margin-top:40px; font-size:70%;">무드애드는 <span style="color:#18A8F1;">아무 업체와 계약을 맺지 않습니다.</span></span></h2>
<p>대표님의 성공이 곧 저희의 성공이기에 조건에 맞지 않는 업체는 정중히 사양하겠습니다.</p><br/><br/>

    let timer = null;
    let innerTimers = [];
    let idx = 0;
    const SPEED = 0.8;

    const speedMs = (n) => Math.max(60, Math.round(n * SPEED));
    const speedSec = (n) => (n * SPEED).toFixed(3);

    function setBg(bg){
      shell.classList.remove('bg-paper','bg-black','bg-mood');
      shell.classList.add('bg-' + bg);
    }

    function clearTimers(){
      clearTimeout(timer);
      innerTimers.forEach(clearTimeout);
      innerTimers = [];
    }

    function delay(fn, ms){
      const t = setTimeout(fn, speedMs(ms));
      innerTimers.push(t);
      return t;
    }

    function baseScene(){
      const el = document.createElement('div');
      el.className = 'scene';
      return el;
    }

    function plainScene(item){
      const s = baseScene();
      s.innerHTML = `<div class="copy ${item.size || 'xl'} ${item.color || 'ink'} ${item.motion || 'motion-rise'}">${item.text}</div>`;
      return s;
    }

    function typeScene(item){
      const s = baseScene();
      s.innerHTML = `<div class="type-wrap"><div class="type-line" style="--chars:${item.chars || item.text.length};--typing:${speedSec(Math.max(.62, item.text.length * .1))}s">${item.text}</div></div>`;
      s._start = () => requestAnimationFrame(() => s.querySelector('.type-line').classList.add('typing'));
      return s;
    }

    function questionScene(item){
      const s = baseScene();
      s.innerHTML = `<div class="question yellow"><span class="q-outer"><span class="q-inner">${item.text}</span></span><span class="emoji">😢</span></div>`;
      return s;
    }

    function exposureOnlyScene(item){
      const s = baseScene();
      s.innerHTML = `
        <div class="exposure-scene">
          <span class="full-screen-x" aria-hidden="true">
            <span class="stroke s1"></span>
            <span class="stroke s2"></span>
          </span>
          <div class="exposure-line">
            <span>노출</span>
            <span>${item.tail}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      `;
      return s;
    }

    function persuadeScene(item){
      const s = baseScene();
      s.innerHTML = `<div class="persuade-scene"><div class="persuade-panel"></div><div class="persuade-word">${item.text}</div></div>`;
      return s;
    }

    function insertScene(item){
      const s = baseScene();
      s.innerHTML = `<div class="insert-scene"><div class="insert-base">${item.before}<span class="insert-hole"><span class="insert-word">${item.insert}</span></span>${item.after}</div></div>`;
      s._start = () => delay(() => s.querySelector('.insert-word').classList.add('pop'), 120);
      return s;
    }

    function mediaScene(item){
      const s = baseScene();
      s.innerHTML = `<div class="media-scene"><div class="media-card ${item.theme || ''}"><div class="mock-bg"></div><div class="media-frame"></div><div class="media-lines"></div><div class="media-scan"></div><div class="media-mini">${item.tag || ''}</div><div class="media-label">${item.label}</div></div></div>`;

    }

      s._start = () => {
        delay(() => s.querySelector('.star-meter').classList.add('fill'), 60);
        delay(() => {
          const el = s.querySelector('.score-num');
          const target = parseFloat(item.score || '4.98');
          const duration = speedMs(1180);
          const start = performance.now();
          function tick(now){
            const p = Math.min(1, (now - start) / duration);
            el.textContent = (target * p).toFixed(2);
            if(p < 1) requestAnimationFrame(tick);
          }
          requestAnimationFrame(tick);
        }, 120);
      };
      return s;
    }

    function realCameraScene(){
      const s = baseScene();

      s.innerHTML = `
        <div class="camera-field-wrap">
          <div class="camera-field-rig" id="cameraFieldRig">
            <div class="field-word size-l w1">네이버 플레이스</div>
            <div class="field-word size-m w2">체험단</div>
            <div class="field-word size-m w3">기자단</div>
            <div class="field-word size-l w4">SNS 컨텐츠</div>
            <div class="field-word size-l w5">검색광고</div>
            <div class="field-word size-m w6">리워드 트래픽</div>
            <div class="field-word size-l w7">브랜드 블로그</div>
          </div>
          <div class="camera-vignette"></div>
        </div>
      `;

      s._start = () => {
        const rig = s.querySelector('#cameraFieldRig');
        const words = Array.from(s.querySelectorAll('.field-word'));
        const isMobile = window.innerWidth <= 820;

        const rigCenterX = isMobile ? 560 : 800;
        const rigCenterY = isMobile ? 410 : 490;

        const focusAnchorX = rigCenterX;
        const focusAnchorY = rigCenterY - (isMobile ? 68 : 92);

       const shots = isMobile
  ? [
      { focus:0, scale:1.26, arcX:-20, arcY:-8, hold:760 },
      { focus:1, scale:1.52, arcX:20, arcY:-10, hold:760 },
      { focus:2, scale:1.54, arcX:24, arcY:6, hold:760 },
      { focus:3, scale:1.34, arcX:8, arcY:16, hold:760 },
      { focus:4, scale:1.38, arcX:-18, arcY:16, hold:760 },
      { focus:5, scale:1.44, arcX:-10, arcY:-16, hold:760 },
      { focus:6, scale:1.26, arcX:18, arcY:16, hold:260 }
    ]
  : [
      { focus:0, scale:1.10, arcX:-34, arcY:-14, hold:760 },
      { focus:1, scale:1.28, arcX:34, arcY:-14, hold:760 },
      { focus:2, scale:1.30, arcX:38, arcY:8, hold:760 },
      { focus:3, scale:1.14, arcX:12, arcY:20, hold:760 },
      { focus:4, scale:1.16, arcX:-28, arcY:18, hold:760 },
      { focus:5, scale:1.22, arcX:-12, arcY:-24, hold:760 },
      { focus:6, scale:1.10, arcX:28, arcY:20, hold:240 }
    ];

        let currentTransform = {
          tx: 0,
          ty: 0,
          scale: isMobile ? 0.98 : 0.96
        };

        function setWordStates(focusIndex){
          words.forEach((word, idx) => {
            word.classList.remove('focus', 'echo', 'hiddenish');

            if(idx === focusIndex){
              word.classList.add('focus');
            } else if(idx < focusIndex){
              word.classList.add('echo');
            } else {
              word.classList.add('hiddenish');
            }
          });
        }

        function setTransform(tx, ty, scale, noTransition = false){
          if(noTransition){
            rig.style.transition = 'none';
          } else {
            rig.style.transition = 'transform 1.05s cubic-bezier(.16,.94,.18,1), filter .45s ease';
          }
          rig.style.transform = `translate(-50%, -50%) translate(${tx}px, ${ty}px) scale(${scale})`;
          currentTransform = { tx, ty, scale };
        }

        function getWordCenter(word){
          return {
            x: word.offsetLeft + (word.offsetWidth / 2),
            y: word.offsetTop + (word.offsetHeight / 2)
          };
        }

        function moveToShot(shot){
          const targetWord = words[shot.focus];
          const center = getWordCenter(targetWord);

          const targetTx = focusAnchorX - center.x;
          const targetTy = focusAnchorY - center.y;

          const startTx = currentTransform.tx - shot.arcX;
          const startTy = currentTransform.ty - shot.arcY;
          const startScale = Math.max((currentTransform.scale || 1) * 0.965, isMobile ? 0.92 : 0.90);

          rig.classList.remove('arc-move');
          void rig.offsetWidth;
          rig.classList.add('arc-move');

          setTransform(startTx, startTy, startScale, true);

          requestAnimationFrame(() => {
            requestAnimationFrame(() => {
              setTransform(targetTx, targetTy, shot.scale, false);
            });
          });

          setWordStates(shot.focus);
        }

        let idxShot = 0;
        setWordStates(0);
        moveToShot(shots[0]);

        function nextShot(){
          idxShot += 1;
          if(idxShot >= shots.length) return;
          moveToShot(shots[idxShot]);
          delay(nextShot, shots[idxShot].hold || 760);
        }

        delay(nextShot, shots[0].hold || 760);
      };

      return s;
    }

    function stairScene(){
      const s = baseScene();
      s.innerHTML = `
        <div class="step-photo-scene">
          <div class="step-line l1"><span class="step-outline">많이</span><span class="step-fill">해봤고</span></div>
          <div class="step-line l2"><span class="step-outline">많이</span><span class="step-fill">해봤고</span></div>
          <div class="step-line l3"><span class="step-outline">많이</span><span class="step-fill">해봤고</span></div>
        </div>
      `;
      return s;
    }

    function highlightTypeScene(item){
      const s = baseScene();
      s.classList.add('type-mode');
      s.innerHTML = `<div class="highlight-scene type-mode"><div class="highlight-card"><div class="highlight-copy" style="--chars:${item.chars || item.text.length};--typing:${speedSec(.72)}s">${item.text}</div></div></div>`;
      s._start = () => requestAnimationFrame(() => s.querySelector('.highlight-scene').classList.add('show'));
      return s;
    }

    function finalScene(item){
      const s = baseScene();
      s.innerHTML = `
        <div class="final-clean">
          <div class="final-glow"></div>
          <div class="final-brand-kor">${item.text}</div>
          <div class="final-brand-eng">MOODAD</div>
        </div>
      `;
      return s;
    }

    function buildScene(item){
      if(item.type === 'plain') return plainScene(item);
      if(item.type === 'type') return typeScene(item);
      if(item.type === 'question') return questionScene(item);
      if(item.type === 'exposureOnly') return exposureOnlyScene(item);
      if(item.type === 'persuade') return persuadeScene(item);
      if(item.type === 'insert') return insertScene(item);
      if(item.type === 'media') return mediaScene(item);
      if(item.type === 'longword') return longwordScene(item);
      if(item.type === 'satisfaction') return satisfactionScene(item);
      if(item.type === 'realCamera') return realCameraScene();
      if(item.type === 'stair') return stairScene();
      if(item.type === 'highlightType') return highlightTypeScene(item);
      if(item.type === 'final') return finalScene(item);
      return plainScene(item);
    }

    let heroLoopEnabled = true;

    function play(index){
      if(!heroLoopEnabled) return;
      clearTimers();
      const item = sequence[index];
      setBg(item.bg);
      stage.innerHTML = '';

      const scene = buildScene(item);
      stage.appendChild(scene);

      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        if(!heroLoopEnabled) return;
        scene.classList.add('show');
        if(typeof scene._start === 'function') scene._start();
      });

      timer = setTimeout(() => {
        if(!heroLoopEnabled) return;
        scene.classList.add('hide');
        setTimeout(() => {
          if(!heroLoopEnabled) return;
          idx = (index + 1) % sequence.length;
          play(idx);
        }, speedMs(120));
      }, speedMs(item.duration || 900));
    }

    function stopHeroLoop(){
      heroLoopEnabled = false;
      clearTimers();
    }

    function startHeroLoop(){
      if(heroLoopEnabled) return;
      heroLoopEnabled = true;
      play(idx);
    }

    const heroShellEl = document.getElementById('heroShell');

    if (heroShellEl && 'IntersectionObserver' in window) {
      const heroVisibilityObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.forEach((entry) => {
          if (entry.isIntersecting && !document.hidden) {
            startHeroLoop();
          } else {
            stopHeroLoop();
          }
        });
      }, { threshold: 0.08 });

      heroVisibilityObserver.observe(heroShellEl);
    }

    document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', () => {
      if (document.hidden) {
        stopHeroLoop();
      } else if (heroShellEl) {
        const rect = heroShellEl.getBoundingClientRect();
        const isVisible = rect.bottom > 0 && rect.top < window.innerHeight;
        if (isVisible) startHeroLoop();
      }
    });

    play(0);
  
</script>
<script>

    const topbar = document.querySelector('.topbar');
    const revealItems = document.querySelectorAll('.reveal');
    const motionItems = document.querySelectorAll('.service-wide');

    let ticking = false;

    function onScroll() {
      if (!ticking) {
        window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
          const triggerSection = document.querySelector('.hero');
          const triggerPoint = triggerSection ? Math.max(triggerSection.offsetTop - 20, 10) : 10;
          if (window.scrollY >= triggerPoint) {
            topbar.classList.add('scrolled');
          } else {
            topbar.classList.remove('scrolled');
          }
          ticking = false;
        });
        ticking = true;
      }
    }

    window.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, { passive: true });

    const revealObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
      entries.forEach((entry) => {
        if (entry.isIntersecting) {
          entry.target.classList.add('show');
        } else {
          entry.target.classList.remove('show');
        }
      });
    }, {
      threshold: 0.16,
      rootMargin: '0px 0px -8% 0px'
    });

    revealItems.forEach((item, index) => {
      let delay = `${Math.min((index % 4) * 0.08, 0.24)}s`;

      if (item.classList.contains('reveal-late')) {
        delay = '0.48s';
        item.style.transitionDuration = '1.3s';
      }

      if (item.classList.contains('reveal-rise-slow')) {
        delay = '0.22s';
        item.style.transitionDuration = '1.35s';
      }

      item.style.transitionDelay = delay;
      revealObserver.observe(item);
    });

    motionItems.forEach((item, index) => {
      item.style.transitionDelay = `${Math.min(index * 0.05, 0.2)}s`;
      revealObserver.observe(item);
    });



    const processTimeline = document.querySelector('.process-timeline');
    const processSteps = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.process-step'));

    function clamp(value, min, max) {
      return Math.min(Math.max(value, min), max);
    }

    function getNodeTargetTop(stepEl, nodeEl, targetEl = null) {
      if (!stepEl || !nodeEl) return 0;
      const baseEl = targetEl || stepEl.querySelector('.process-card');
      if (!baseEl) return 0;
      const stepRect = stepEl.getBoundingClientRect();
      const baseRect = baseEl.getBoundingClientRect();
      return (baseRect.top - stepRect.top) + (baseRect.height / 2) - (nodeEl.offsetHeight / 2);
    }

    function updateProcessNodes() {
      if (!processTimeline || !processSteps.length) return;

      if (window.innerWidth <= 980) {
        processSteps.forEach((stepEl) => {
          const nodeEl = stepEl.querySelector('.process-node');
          if (!nodeEl) return;
          nodeEl.style.removeProperty('--node-top');
        });
        return;
      }

      processSteps.forEach((stepEl) => {
        const nodeEl = stepEl.querySelector('.process-node');
        if (!nodeEl) return;

        const targetTop = getNodeTargetTop(stepEl, nodeEl);
        const stepRect = stepEl.getBoundingClientRect();
        const stepTop = stepRect.top + window.scrollY;
        const start = stepTop - (window.innerHeight * 0.9);
        const end = stepTop - (window.innerHeight * 0.28);
        const progress = clamp((window.scrollY - start) / Math.max(end - start, 1), 0, 1);
        const currentTop = targetTop * progress;

        nodeEl.style.setProperty('--node-top', `${currentTop.toFixed(1)}px`);
      });
    }

    let processNodeRaf = null;

    function requestProcessNodesUpdate() {
      if (processNodeRaf) return;
      processNodeRaf = window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        processNodeRaf = null;
        updateProcessNodes();
      });
    }

    window.addEventListener('scroll', requestProcessNodesUpdate, { passive: true });
    window.addEventListener('resize', requestProcessNodesUpdate);
    window.addEventListener('load', requestProcessNodesUpdate);
    requestProcessNodesUpdate();


    // Hero 두 줄 타이핑
    const typingLine1 = document.querySelector('#typing-line-1');
    const typingLine2 = document.querySelector('#typing-line-2');

    if (typingLine1 && typingLine2) {
      const line2Segments = [
        { text: '진짜 관리를', color: '#6aaaf0', weight: '900' },
        { text: '시작합니다.', color: '#000000', weight: '900' }
      ];

      let startedTyping = false;

      function typeSegments(target, segments, speed = 70) {
        return new Promise((resolve) => {
          let segmentIndex = 0;
          let charIndex = 0;
          let currentSpan = null;

          function step() {
            if (segmentIndex >= segments.length) {
              resolve();
              return;
            }

            const segment = segments[segmentIndex];

            if (!currentSpan) {
              currentSpan = document.createElement('span');
              currentSpan.style.color = segment.color;
              currentSpan.style.fontWeight = segment.weight;
              currentSpan.classList.add('typing-cursor');
              target.appendChild(currentSpan);
            }

            currentSpan.textContent += segment.text.charAt(charIndex);
            charIndex++;

            if (charIndex >= segment.text.length) {
              currentSpan.classList.remove('typing-cursor');
              currentSpan = null;
              charIndex = 0;
              segmentIndex++;
            }

            setTimeout(step, speed);
          }

          step();
        });
      }

      async function runHeroTyping() {
        typingLine1.innerHTML = '';
        typingLine1.textContent = '95%의 대행사가 포기한';
        typingLine2.innerHTML = '';
        await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, 180));
        await typeSegments(typingLine2, line2Segments, 75);
      }

      const typingObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.forEach((entry) => {
          if (entry.isIntersecting && !startedTyping) {
            startedTyping = true;
            runHeroTyping();
            typingObserver.disconnect();
          }
        });
      }, {
        threshold: 0.45
      });

      typingObserver.observe(typingLine1);
    }

    const servicesTypingLine1 = document.querySelector('#services-typing-line-1');
    const servicesTypingLine2 = document.querySelector('#services-typing-line-2');

    if (servicesTypingLine1 && servicesTypingLine2) {
      const servicesLine1Text = '매출 폭주를 막을 수 없는';
      const servicesLine2Text = '6가지 전략';
      let servicesTypingStarted = false;

      function setupServicesTypingLine(target, text) {
        target.innerHTML = '';

        const preview = document.createElement('span');
        preview.className = 'typing-preview';
        preview.textContent = text;

        const live = document.createElement('span');
        live.className = 'typing-live';
        live.textContent = '';

        target.appendChild(preview);
        target.appendChild(live);

        return live;
      }

      const servicesTypingLive1 = setupServicesTypingLine(servicesTypingLine1, servicesLine1Text);
      const servicesTypingLive2 = setupServicesTypingLine(servicesTypingLine2, servicesLine2Text);

      function typeSingleLine(target, liveTarget, text, speed = 82) {
        return new Promise((resolve) => {
          let index = 0;
          liveTarget.textContent = '';
          target.classList.add('services-typing-cursor');

          function step() {
            liveTarget.textContent += text.charAt(index);
            index += 1;

            if (index < text.length) {
              setTimeout(step, speed);
            } else {
              target.classList.remove('services-typing-cursor');
              resolve();
            }
          }

          if (!text.length) {
            target.classList.remove('services-typing-cursor');
            resolve();
            return;
          }

          step();
        });
      }

      async function runServicesTyping() {
        await typeSingleLine(servicesTypingLine1, servicesTypingLive1, servicesLine1Text, 68);
        await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, 180));
        await typeSingleLine(servicesTypingLine2, servicesTypingLive2, servicesLine2Text, 90);
      }

      const servicesTypingObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.forEach((entry) => {
          if (entry.isIntersecting && !servicesTypingStarted) {
            servicesTypingStarted = true;
            runServicesTyping();
            servicesTypingObserver.disconnect();
          }
        });
      }, {
        threshold: 0.4
      });

      servicesTypingObserver.observe(servicesTypingLine1);
    }

    // ===== 후기 슬라이드 섹션 재구성 시작 =====
    // 아래 reviews 배열의 thumb / original 경로만 나중에 바꿔서 사용하시면 됩니다.
    const reviews = [
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-01.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-01.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-02.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-02.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-03.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-03.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-04.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-04.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-05.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-05.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-06.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-06.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-07.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-07.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-08.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-08.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-09.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-09.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-10.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-10.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-11.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-11.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-12.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-12.jpg' },
  { thumb: 'reviews/review-thumb-13.jpg', original: 'reviews/review-original-13.jpg' }
];

    const reviewsRowTop = document.getElementById('reviewsRowTop');
    const reviewsRowBottom = document.getElementById('reviewsRowBottom');
    const reviewsModal = document.getElementById('reviewsModal');
    const reviewsModalImage = document.getElementById('reviewsModalImage');
    const reviewsModalOverlay = document.getElementById('reviewsModalOverlay');

    function createReviewTrack(items) {
      const track = document.createElement('div');
      track.className = 'reviews-row-track';

      items.forEach((item, index) => {
        const card = document.createElement('button');
        card.type = 'button';
        card.className = 'reviews-slide-card';
        card.setAttribute('aria-label', `후기 이미지 ${index + 1} 크게 보기`);

        const image = document.createElement('img');
        image.src = item.thumb;         // 슬라이드에는 요약본 경로 사용
        image.alt = `후기 요약본 ${index + 1}`;
        image.dataset.origin = item.original;  // 클릭 시 원본 경로 사용

        card.appendChild(image);
        track.appendChild(card);
      });

      return track;
    }

    if (reviewsRowTop && reviewsRowBottom) {
      const duplicatedTop = [...reviews, ...reviews];
      const duplicatedBottom = [...reviews.slice().reverse(), ...reviews.slice().reverse()];

      reviewsRowTop.appendChild(createReviewTrack(duplicatedTop));
      reviewsRowBottom.appendChild(createReviewTrack(duplicatedBottom));
    }

    function openReviewsModal(originSrc) {
      if (!reviewsModal || !reviewsModalImage) return;
      reviewsModalImage.src = originSrc;
      reviewsModal.classList.add('is-open');
      reviewsModal.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    }

    function closeReviewsModal() {
      if (!reviewsModal || !reviewsModalImage) return;
      reviewsModal.classList.remove('is-open');
      reviewsModal.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
      document.body.style.overflow = '';
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (!reviewsModal.classList.contains('is-open')) {
          reviewsModalImage.src = '';
        }
      }, 220);
    }

    document.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
      const targetImage = event.target.closest('.reviews-slide-card img');

      if (!targetImage || !targetImage.dataset.origin) return;

      if (reviewsModal && reviewsModal.classList.contains('is-open')) {
        closeReviewsModal();
        return;
      }

      openReviewsModal(targetImage.dataset.origin);
    });

    if (reviewsModalOverlay) {
      reviewsModalOverlay.addEventListener('click', closeReviewsModal);
    }

    if (reviewsModal) {
      reviewsModal.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
        if (!reviewsModal.classList.contains('is-open')) return;
        closeReviewsModal();
      });
    }

    if (reviewsModalImage) {
      reviewsModalImage.addEventListener('click', closeReviewsModal);
    }

    document.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Escape' && reviewsModal && reviewsModal.classList.contains('is-open')) {
        closeReviewsModal();
      }
    });
    // ===== 후기 슬라이드 섹션 재구성 끝 =====

  
</script>
<script>

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  const problemPanels = document.querySelectorAll(".problem-panel");
  if (problemPanels.length) {
    problemPanels.forEach((panel) => {
      panel.addEventListener("mouseenter", () => {
        if (window.innerWidth <= 920) return;
        problemPanels.forEach((p) => p.classList.remove("is-active"));
        panel.classList.add("is-active");
      });
      panel.addEventListener("focusin", () => {
        if (window.innerWidth <= 920) return;
        problemPanels.forEach((p) => p.classList.remove("is-active"));
        panel.classList.add("is-active");
      });
    });
  }
});

</script>

<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
    const panels = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.problem-panel'));
    if (!panels.length) return;

    function setMobileActive(nextPanel){
      panels.forEach((panel, index) => {
        panel.classList.toggle('is-active', panel === nextPanel);
        panel.setAttribute('aria-expanded', panel === nextPanel ? 'true' : 'false');
      });
    }

    function applyProblemMode(){
      if (window.innerWidth <= 920) {
        const alreadyActive = panels.find(panel => panel.classList.contains('is-active'));
        setMobileActive(alreadyActive || panels[0]);
      } else {
        panels.forEach(panel => panel.setAttribute('aria-expanded', panel.classList.contains('is-active') ? 'true' : 'false'));
      }
    }

    panels.forEach((panel, index) => {
      panel.setAttribute('tabindex', '0');
      panel.addEventListener('click', function(){
        if (window.innerWidth > 920) return;
        if (!panel.classList.contains('is-active')) setMobileActive(panel);
      });
      panel.addEventListener('keydown', function(e){
        if (window.innerWidth > 920) return;
        if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
          e.preventDefault();
          setMobileActive(panel);
        }
      });
    });

    applyProblemMode();
    window.addEventListener('resize', applyProblemMode);
  });
</script>

<script>
(function(){
  const mobileSteps = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.reveal-mobile-step'));
  const editorial = document.querySelector('.mobile-process-editorial');
  const connectors = editorial ? Array.from(editorial.querySelectorAll('.mobile-step-connector')) : [];
  if(!editorial || !connectors.length || !mobileSteps.length) return;

  const mq = window.matchMedia('(max-width: 920px)');

  function clamp(value, min, max){
    return Math.min(Math.max(value, min), max);
  }

  function updateConnectors(){
    if(!mq.matches) return;

    const viewportTrigger = window.innerHeight * 0.42;

    mobileSteps.forEach((step, index) => {
      if(step.getBoundingClientRect().top < window.innerHeight * 0.86){
        step.classList.add('inview');
      }
      step.classList.remove('is-active');

      const connector = connectors[index];
      if(!connector) return;

      const orb = connector.querySelector('.mobile-step-connector-orb');
      const currentCard = step.querySelector('.mobile-step-card');
      const nextCard = mobileSteps[index + 1].querySelector('.mobile-step-card');
      const connectorRect = connector.getBoundingClientRect();
      const currentRect = currentCard.getBoundingClientRect();
      const nextRect = nextCard.getBoundingClientRect();
      const orbSize = orb.offsetHeight || 34;
      const maxTravel = Math.max(connector.clientHeight - orbSize, 0);

      const startPoint = currentRect.bottom;
      const endPoint = nextRect.top;
      const progress = clamp((viewportTrigger - startPoint) / Math.max(endPoint - startPoint, 1), 0, 1);
      const orbTop = maxTravel * progress;

      orb.style.top = `${orbTop.toFixed(1)}px`;

      if(progress > 0.02 && progress < 0.98){
        step.classList.add('is-active');
        mobileSteps[index + 1].classList.add('is-active');
      } else if(progress >= 0.98){
        mobileSteps[index + 1].classList.add('is-active');
      } else if(index === 0 && viewportTrigger < startPoint){
        step.classList.add('is-active');
      }

      const lineTop = currentRect.bottom - connectorRect.top;
      const lineBottom = nextRect.top - connectorRect.top;
      const track = connector.querySelector('.mobile-step-connector-track');
      track.style.top = `${Math.max(0, Math.min(lineTop, connector.clientHeight)).toFixed(1)}px`;
      track.style.height = `${Math.max(0, Math.min(lineBottom, connector.clientHeight) - Math.max(0, Math.min(lineTop, connector.clientHeight))).toFixed(1)}px`;
    });
  }

  let ticking = false;
  function requestUpdate(){
    if(ticking) return;
    ticking = true;
    window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      updateConnectors();
      ticking = false;
    });
  }

  const io = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
    entries.forEach((entry) => {
      if(entry.isIntersecting){
        entry.target.classList.add('inview');
      }
    });
  }, { threshold: 0.18, rootMargin: '0px 0px -10% 0px' });

  mobileSteps.forEach((step) => io.observe(step));
  window.addEventListener('scroll', requestUpdate, { passive:true });
  window.addEventListener('resize', requestUpdate);
  window.addEventListener('load', requestUpdate);
  if(mq.addEventListener){
    mq.addEventListener('change', requestUpdate);
  } else if(mq.addListener){
    mq.addListener(requestUpdate);
  }
  requestUpdate();
})();
</script>

<script id="mobile-hero-overlay-only-script">
(function() {
  function applyMobileHeroOverlayOnly() {
    if (window.innerWidth > 820) return;

    var line1 = document.getElementById('typing-line-1');
    var desc = document.querySelector('.hero-desc');

    if (line1) {
      line1.innerHTML = '';
      line1.textContent = '95%의 대행사가 포기한';
    }

    if (desc) {
      desc.innerHTML = '수백 개 업체를 기계적으로 관리하는<br><strong>획일된 방식은 거부합니다.</strong><br><br>한 팀의 성과에 집착하기 위해,<br>정해진 <strong>소수에게만 집중합니다.</strong>';
    }
  }

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', applyMobileHeroOverlayOnly, { once: true });
  } else {
    applyMobileHeroOverlayOnly();
  }

  window.addEventListener('load', applyMobileHeroOverlayOnly, { once: true });
})();
</script>

<script id="mobile-hero-final-copy-lock">
(function() {
  function lockMobileHeroCopy() {
    if (window.innerWidth > 820) return;

    var line1 = document.getElementById('typing-line-1');
    var desc = document.querySelector('.hero-desc');

    if (line1) {
      line1.innerHTML = '';
      line1.textContent = '95%의 대행사가 포기한';
    }

    if (desc) {
      desc.innerHTML = '수백 개 업체를 기계적으로 관리하는<br><strong>획일된 방식은 거부합니다.</strong><br><br>한 팀의 성과에 집착하기 위해,<br>정해진 <strong>소수에게만 집중합니다.</strong>';
    }
  }

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', lockMobileHeroCopy, { once: true });
  } else {
    lockMobileHeroCopy();
  }

  window.addEventListener('load', lockMobileHeroCopy, { once: true });
  window.addEventListener('resize', lockMobileHeroCopy);
})();
</script>
